\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Main\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Email
\item Phone Third-\/party\+:
\item QQ
\item Weibo
\item We\+Chat
\item Facebook
\item Twitter
\item Google
\item Apple\+ID Other\+:
\item UID (for advance usage)
\item Anonymous
\item QRCode
\end{DoxyItemize}

For email and phone account, usually we need to send a verify code to continue the following steps.

For uid account, it is designed for developers who already has the account system for their own. The developer can register the uid account without any verification. So please keep your username/password in safe place.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Thing server have many regions over the world, China/\+Europe/\+America, and so on. Account system between regions are separated. When user is not logged in, Thing SDK will select a nearest region for the initial API request. During the register step, Thing Cloud will see the account country code and create it in the right region. After the register or login step, the API request will be sent to the right region. So, the country code is part of the account username, please do not ignore it. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ (void) login\+By\+Auth2\+With\+Type\+: \begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(\mbox{\hyperlink{ios-arm64__x86__64-simulator_2_thing_smart_base_kit_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_smart_user_8h_aa390b5d40ea644d8d3cd705b47598860}{Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+Type}})}]{type }\item[{country\+Code\+:(NSString $\ast$)}]{country\+Code }\item[{access\+Token\+:(NSString $\ast$)}]{access\+Token }\item[{extra\+Info\+:(NSDictionary $\ast$)}]{extra\+Info }\item[{success\+:(nullable \mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_ae3aa9bacb5c7dc6f20e04b208db97afb}{Thing\+Success\+Handler}})}]{success }\item[{failure\+:(nullable \mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_af2b46bef0575729ec6391704cfc8a038}{Thing\+Failure\+Error}})}]{failure }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Enables login with a third-\/party account. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em type} & The login type, such as {\ttfamily Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+Type\+Apple} for Apple login. \\
\hline
{\em country\+Code} & The country code. \\
\hline
{\em access\+Token} & The access token for third-\/party account login. \\
\hline
{\em extra\+Info} & Additional parameters containing platform identifier and unique ID for cryptographic tokens. If {\ttfamily type} is {\ttfamily Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+Type\+JWT}, also can use {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_user_login_j_w_t_model}{Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+JWTModel}}}in params extra\+Info. \\
\hline
{\em success} & Called upon successful completion of the task. \\
\hline
{\em failure} & Called when the task fails due to an error. Error domian is {\ttfamily Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+Error\+Domain}, error code is {\ttfamily Thing\+Smart\+User\+Login\+Error\+Code} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{interface_thing_smart_user_ab96a78309ad3ac69ed3cdf11fa859d13}\label{interface_thing_smart_user_ab96a78309ad3ac69ed3cdf11fa859d13}} 
\index{ThingSmartUser@{ThingSmartUser}!switchUserRegion:success:failure:@{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}}
\index{switchUserRegion:success:failure:@{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}!ThingSmartUser@{ThingSmartUser}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ (void) switch\+User\+Region\+: \begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(NSString $\ast$)}]{region }\item[{success\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_ae3aa9bacb5c7dc6f20e04b208db97afb}{Thing\+Success\+Handler}})}]{success }\item[{failure\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_af2b46bef0575729ec6391704cfc8a038}{Thing\+Failure\+Error}})}]{failure }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Switches the region of the logged-\/in user. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
1. Switching the user\textquotesingle{}s region is the same as registering in a new account to the region of the user. To comply with GDPR, when the region is switched, the user\textquotesingle{}s device and scene are not taken to the new account. Only the user\textquotesingle{}s information is taken to the new account. 

2. When the account is switched to the new region, the earlier account is only reserved for 30 days and then will be deleted. 

3. After the region is switched, the new account is logged in. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em region} & The region to register the account. Use \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_user}{Thing\+Smart\+User}} region\+List\+With\+Country\+Code\+:success\+:failure\+:\mbox{]} or \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_user}{Thing\+Smart\+User}} get\+Default\+Region\+With\+Country\+Code\+:\mbox{]} to get the region. \\
\hline
{\em success} & Called when the task is finished. \\
\hline
{\em failure} & Called when the task is interrupted by an error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Provided by category \mbox{\hyperlink{category_thing_smart_user_07_region_08_ab96a78309ad3ac69ed3cdf11fa859d13}{Thing\+Smart\+User(\+Region)}}.

\index{switchUserRegion:success:failure:@{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}!ThingSmartUser@{ThingSmartUser}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}{switchUserRegion:success:failure:}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily -\/ (void) switch\+User\+Region\+: \begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(NSString $\ast$)}]{region }\item[{success\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_ae3aa9bacb5c7dc6f20e04b208db97afb}{Thing\+Success\+Handler}})}]{success }\item[{failure\+:(\mbox{\hyperlink{_thing_smart_matter_interface_a_p_i_8framework_2_headers_2_thing_matter_share_interface_a_p_i_8h_af2b46bef0575729ec6391704cfc8a038}{Thing\+Failure\+Error}})}]{failure }\end{DoxyParamCaption}}

Switches the region of the logged-\/in user. \begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
1. Switching the user\textquotesingle{}s region is the same as registering in a new account to the region of the user. To comply with GDPR, when the region is switched, the user\textquotesingle{}s device and scene are not taken to the new account. Only the user\textquotesingle{}s information is taken to the new account. 

2. When the account is switched to the new region, the earlier account is only reserved for 30 days and then will be deleted. 

3. After the region is switched, the new account is logged in. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em region} & The region to register the account. Use \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_user}{Thing\+Smart\+User}} region\+List\+With\+Country\+Code\+:success\+:failure\+:\mbox{]} or \mbox{[}\mbox{\hyperlink{interface_thing_smart_user}{Thing\+Smart\+User}} get\+Default\+Region\+With\+Country\+Code\+:\mbox{]} to get the region. \\
\hline
{\em success} & Called when the task is finished. \\
\hline
{\em failure} & Called when the task is interrupted by an error. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
